broker-side authentication implementation consists of several key components working together in a chain:\\n\\n## Authentication Entry Point\\n\\nThe **ChannelBuilders.serverChannelBuilder()** method (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ChannelBuilders.java) is the primary entry point for creating server-side SASL channel builders. It loads enabled SASL mechanisms from BrokerSecurityConfigs.SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG and creates a SaslChannelBuilder instance with JAAS contexts for each mechanism.\\n\\n## Core SASL Server Authenticator\\n\\nThe **SaslServerAuthenticator** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java) is the main server-side authenticator that:\\n- Manages the SASL handshake protocol (INITIAL_REQUEST, HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST, HANDSHAKE_REQUEST, AUTHENTICATE states)\\n- Selects the appropriate SASL mechanism based on client request\\n- Creates mechanism-specific SaslServer instances via Sasl.createSaslServer()\\n- Handles GSSAPI/Kerberos through createSaslKerberosServer() method\\n- Manages authentication context lifecycle through SaslAuthenticationContext\\n\\n## Mechanism Selection & Configuration\\n\\nThe **SaslChannelBuilder** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java) is responsible for:\\n- Maintaining Maps of enabled SASL mechanisms per listener\\n- Loading JAAS contexts using JaasContext.loadServerContext() for each enabled mechanism (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java)\\n- Mapping mechanism-specific callback handlers\\n- Creating the appropriate callback handler instances based on mechanism type\\n- Managing credential caches for different SASL mechanisms\\n\\nConfiguration is driven by:\\n- **SaslConfigs** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/SaslConfigs.java) - defines SASL_MECHANISM, SASL_JAAS_CONFIG, SASL_CLIENT_CALLBACK_HANDLER_CLASS\\n- **BrokerSecurityConfigs** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/internals/BrokerSecurityConfigs.java) - defines SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG, SASL_SERVER_CALLBACK_HANDLER_CLASS_CONFIG, CONNECTIONS_MAX_REAUTH_MS_CONFIG\\n\\n## PLAIN SASL Mechanism Implementation\\n\\nThe PLAIN mechanism is implemented through:\\n- **PlainSaslServer** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServer.java) - implements SaslServer interface\\n- **PlainSaslServerProvider** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServerProvider.java) - provides factory for PlainSaslServer\\n- **PlainServerCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainServerCallbackHandler.java) - implements AuthenticateCallbackHandler\\n- **PlainLoginModule** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/PlainLoginModule.java) - JAAS login module\\n\\n## SCRAM SASL Mechanism Implementation\\n\\nThe SCRAM mechanisms (SCRAM-SHA-256, SCRAM-SHA-512) are implemented through:\\n- **ScramSaslServer** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServer.java) - implements SaslServer interface, handles SCRAM protocol exchange\\n- **ScramSaslServerProvider** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServerProvider.java) - factory for both SCRAM-SHA-256 and SCRAM-SHA-512\\n- **ScramServerCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java) - implements AuthenticateCallbackHandler\\n- **ScramMechanism** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMechanism.java) - enum defining SCRAM_SHA_256 and SCRAM_SHA_512\\n- **ScramFormatter** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramFormatter.java) - handles SCRAM credential generation\\n- **ScramMessages** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMessages.java) - SCRAM protocol message handling\\n- **ScramCredentialUtils** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramCredentialUtils.java) - utilities for credential cache creation\\n- **ScramLoginModule** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramLoginModule.java) - JAAS login module\\n- **ScramCredential** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredential.java) - credential data class\\n\\n## GSSAPI/Kerberos SASL Mechanism Implementation\\n\\nGSSAPI (Kerberos) is handled by:\\n- **SaslServerAuthenticator.createSaslKerberosServer()** - creates Kerberos SaslServer\\n- **DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder.java) - extracts principal from Kerberos authentication\\n- Kerberos-specific JAAS context loading in SaslChannelBuilder\\n\\n## Authentication Context Lifecycle\\n\\nThe **SaslAuthenticationContext** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslAuthenticationContext.java) manages:\\n- Stores the SaslServer instance\\n- Maintains SecurityProtocol and client address information\\n- Implements the **AuthenticationContext** interface (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/AuthenticationContext.java)\\n- Tracks listener name and optional TLS session information\\n- Lifecycle: created during handshake, used for principal extraction, closed after authentication\\n\\n## Callback Handler Infrastructure\\n\\n**AuthenticateCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/AuthenticateCallbackHandler.java) is the base interface that all server callback handlers implement. **SaslServerCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerCallbackHandler.java) provides default handling for:\\n- RealmCallback\\n- AuthorizeCallback (for GSSAPI)\\n- Custom mechanism-specific callbacks\\n\\n## Credential Management\\n\\n**CredentialCache** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/CredentialCache.java) manages credentials per mechanism:\\n- SCRAM credentials stored and retrieved by username\\n- **ScramCredentialCallback** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredentialCallback.java) allows callback handlers to access credentials\\n- **DelegationTokenCache** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/token/delegation/internals/DelegationTokenCache.java) manages delegation token credentials\\n- **CredentialProvider** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/CredentialProvider.java) coordinates cache management\\n\\n## SASL Protocol Messages\\n\\nThe SASL handshake and authentication use Kafka protocol messages:\\n- **SaslHandshakeRequest/Response** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/SaslHandshakeRequest.java, Response.java) - mechanism negotiation\\n- **SaslAuthenticateRequest/Response** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/SaslAuthenticateRequest.java, Response.java) - mechanism-specific tokens\\n- **SaslExtensions/SaslExtensionsCallback** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslExtensions*.java) - mechanism extensions\\n\\n## JAAS Integration\\n\\n**JaasContext** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java) provides:\\n- loadServerContext() - loads server JAAS configuration for specific listener and mechanism\\n- Configuration entry management from JAAS config files or dynamic configuration\\n- **LoginManager** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/LoginManager.java) - manages login lifecycle per mechanism\\n- **AbstractLogin/DefaultLogin** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/AbstractLogin.java, DefaultLogin.java) - login implementations\\n\\n## Additional SASL Mechanism (OAuth Bearer)\\n\\n**OAuthBearerSaslServer** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/OAuthBearerSaslServer.java) and **OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler.java) implement OAuth Bearer token authentication.\\n\\n## Error Handling\\n\\n**SaslAuthenticationException** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/errors/SaslAuthenticationException.java) is thrown for SASL-specific authentication failures.\\n\\n## Configuration & Internal Details\\n\\n**SaslInternalConfigs** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslInternalConfigs.java) defines internal SASL configuration like credential lifetime management for session-based reauthentication.\\n\\nThe complete authentication flow: Client connects → ChannelBuilders creates SaslChannelBuilder → SaslChannelBuilder creates SaslServerAuthenticator → SaslServerAuthenticator performs handshake → mechanism selected → appropriate SaslServer created (PLAIN/SCRAM/GSSAPI) → SaslAuthenticationContext established → credentials validated via callbacks → authentication broker-side authentication implementation consists of several key components working together in a chain:\\n\\n## Authentication Entry Point\\n\\nThe **ChannelBuilders.serverChannelBuilder()** method (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ChannelBuilders.java) is the primary entry point for creating server-side SASL channel builders. It loads enabled SASL mechanisms from BrokerSecurityConfigs.SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG and creates a SaslChannelBuilder instance with JAAS contexts for each mechanism.\\n\\n## Core SASL Server Authenticator\\n\\nThe **SaslServerAuthenticator** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java) is the main server-side authenticator that:\\n- Manages the SASL handshake protocol (INITIAL_REQUEST, HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST, HANDSHAKE_REQUEST, AUTHENTICATE states)\\n- Selects the appropriate SASL mechanism based on client request\\n- Creates mechanism-specific SaslServer instances via Sasl.createSaslServer()\\n- Handles GSSAPI/Kerberos through createSaslKerberosServer() method\\n- Manages authentication context lifecycle through SaslAuthenticationContext\\n\\n## Mechanism Selection & Configuration\\n\\nThe **SaslChannelBuilder** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java) is responsible for:\\n- Maintaining Maps of enabled SASL mechanisms per listener\\n- Loading JAAS contexts using JaasContext.loadServerContext() for each enabled mechanism (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java)\\n- Mapping mechanism-specific callback handlers\\n- Creating the appropriate callback handler instances based on mechanism type\\n- Managing credential caches for different SASL mechanisms\\n\\nConfiguration is driven by:\\n- **SaslConfigs** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/SaslConfigs.java) - defines SASL_MECHANISM, SASL_JAAS_CONFIG, SASL_CLIENT_CALLBACK_HANDLER_CLASS\\n- **BrokerSecurityConfigs** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/internals/BrokerSecurityConfigs.java) - defines SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG, SASL_SERVER_CALLBACK_HANDLER_CLASS_CONFIG, CONNECTIONS_MAX_REAUTH_MS_CONFIG\\n\\n## PLAIN SASL Mechanism Implementation\\n\\nThe PLAIN mechanism is implemented through:\\n- **PlainSaslServer** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServer.java) - implements SaslServer interface\\n- **PlainSaslServerProvider** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServerProvider.java) - provides factory for PlainSaslServer\\n- **PlainServerCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainServerCallbackHandler.java) - implements AuthenticateCallbackHandler\\n- **PlainLoginModule** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/PlainLoginModule.java) - JAAS login module\\n\\n## SCRAM SASL Mechanism Implementation\\n\\nThe SCRAM mechanisms (SCRAM-SHA-256, SCRAM-SHA-512) are implemented through:\\n- **ScramSaslServer** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServer.java) - implements SaslServer interface, handles SCRAM protocol exchange\\n- **ScramSaslServerProvider** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServerProvider.java) - factory for both SCRAM-SHA-256 and SCRAM-SHA-512\\n- **ScramServerCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java) - implements AuthenticateCallbackHandler\\n- **ScramMechanism** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMechanism.java) - enum defining SCRAM_SHA_256 and SCRAM_SHA_512\\n- **ScramFormatter** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramFormatter.java) - handles SCRAM credential generation\\n- **ScramMessages** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMessages.java) - SCRAM protocol message handling\\n- **ScramCredentialUtils** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramCredentialUtils.java) - utilities for credential cache creation\\n- **ScramLoginModule** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramLoginModule.java) - JAAS login module\\n- **ScramCredential** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredential.java) - credential data class\\n\\n## GSSAPI/Kerberos SASL Mechanism Implementation\\n\\nGSSAPI (Kerberos) is handled by:\\n- **SaslServerAuthenticator.createSaslKerberosServer()** - creates Kerberos SaslServer\\n- **DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder.java) - extracts principal from Kerberos authentication\\n- Kerberos-specific JAAS context loading in SaslChannelBuilder\\n\\n## Authentication Context Lifecycle\\n\\nThe **SaslAuthenticationContext** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslAuthenticationContext.java) manages:\\n- Stores the SaslServer instance\\n- Maintains SecurityProtocol and client address information\\n- Implements the **AuthenticationContext** interface (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/AuthenticationContext.java)\\n- Tracks listener name and optional TLS session information\\n- Lifecycle: created during handshake, used for principal extraction, closed after authentication\\n\\n## Callback Handler Infrastructure\\n\\n**AuthenticateCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/AuthenticateCallbackHandler.java) is the base interface that all server callback handlers implement. **SaslServerCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerCallbackHandler.java) provides default handling for:\\n- RealmCallback\\n- AuthorizeCallback (for GSSAPI)\\n- Custom mechanism-specific callbacks\\n\\n## Credential Management\\n\\n**CredentialCache** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/CredentialCache.java) manages credentials per mechanism:\\n- SCRAM credentials stored and retrieved by username\\n- **ScramCredentialCallback** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredentialCallback.java) allows callback handlers to access credentials\\n- **DelegationTokenCache** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/token/delegation/internals/DelegationTokenCache.java) manages delegation token credentials\\n- **CredentialProvider** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/CredentialProvider.java) coordinates cache management\\n\\n## SASL Protocol Messages\\n\\nThe SASL handshake and authentication use Kafka protocol messages:\\n- **SaslHandshakeRequest/Response** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/SaslHandshakeRequest.java, Response.java) - mechanism negotiation\\n- **SaslAuthenticateRequest/Response** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/SaslAuthenticateRequest.java, Response.java) - mechanism-specific tokens\\n- **SaslExtensions/SaslExtensionsCallback** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslExtensions*.java) - mechanism extensions\\n\\n## JAAS Integration\\n\\n**JaasContext** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java) provides:\\n- loadServerContext() - loads server JAAS configuration for specific listener and mechanism\\n- Configuration entry management from JAAS config files or dynamic configuration\\n- **LoginManager** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/LoginManager.java) - manages login lifecycle per mechanism\\n- **AbstractLogin/DefaultLogin** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/AbstractLogin.java, DefaultLogin.java) - login implementations\\n\\n## Additional SASL Mechanism (OAuth Bearer)\\n\\n**OAuthBearerSaslServer** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/OAuthBearerSaslServer.java) and **OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler.java) implement OAuth Bearer token authentication.\\n\\n## Error Handling\\n\\n**SaslAuthenticationException** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/errors/SaslAuthenticationException.java) is thrown for SASL-specific authentication failures.\\n\\n## Configuration & Internal Details\\n\\n**SaslInternalConfigs** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslInternalConfigs.java) defines internal SASL configuration like credential lifetime management for session-based reauthentication.\\n\\nThe complete authentication flow: Client connects → ChannelBuilders creates SaslChannelBuilder → SaslChannelBuilder creates SaslServerAuthenticator → SaslServerAuthenticator performs handshake → mechanism selected → appropriate SaslServer created (PLAIN/SCRAM/GSSAPI) → SaslAuthenticationContext established → credentials validated via callbacks → authentication complete.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
